<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 1.8pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Abbott Laboratories and Subsidiaries</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 1.8pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 1.8pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to Condensed
Consolidated Financial Statements</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 1.8pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 1.8pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">September 30, 2007</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 1.8pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 1.8pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(Unaudited)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 1.8pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 1.8pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 1 &#151; Basis of
Presentation</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 9.9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 9.9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The accompanying
unaudited, condensed consolidated financial statements have been prepared
pursuant to rules and regulations of the Securities and Exchange Commission
and, therefore, do not include all information and footnote disclosures
normally included in audited financial statements.&#160; However, in the opinion of management, all
adjustments (which include only normal adjustments) necessary to present fairly
the results of operations, financial position and cash flows have been
made.&#160; It is suggested that these
statements be read in conjunction with the financial statements included in
Abbott&#146;s Annual Report on Form 10-K for the year ended December 31, 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 2 &#151; Reclassification
of Assets Previously Classified as Held for Sale</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman"><font style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">On January 17, 2007, the date that
Abbott agreed to sell its core laboratory diagnostics businesses to GE, </font>the
assets of the operations held for sale and the liabilities to be assumed in the
intended sale were classified as held for sale</font><font color="black"><font style="color:windowtext;"> and depreciation of
property and equipment and amortization of intangible assets was
discontinued.&#160; </font>On July 11, 2007,
Abbott announced that Abbott and GE mutually agreed to terminate the contract
to sell Abbott&#146;s core laboratory diagnostics business to GE.&#160; The assets of the operations previously held
for sale and the liabilities to be assumed in the intended sale have been
reclassified to assets held and used.&#160;
Accordingly, </font><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">depreciation and amortization that was discontinued in
the amount of approximately $99 million has been recorded in the third quarter
of 2007.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 3 &#151; Adoption of New
Accounting Standards</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Effective January 1, 2007, Abbott adopted
Statement of Financial Accounting Standards (SFAS) No. 157, &#147;Fair Value
Measurements,&#148; SFAS No. 159, &#147;The Fair Value Option for Financial Assets and
Financial Liabilities,&#148; and FASB Interpretation No. 48, &#147;Accounting for
Uncertainty in Income Taxes.&#148;&#160;&#160; Adoption
of these Standards and Interpretation did not have a material impact on Abbott&#146;s
financial position.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SFAS No. 157 applies to all fair value measurements not otherwise
specified in an existing standard, it clarifies how to measure fair value, and
it expands fair value disclosures.&#160; For
Abbott, SFAS No. 157 does not significantly change the valuation of assets
versus previous practice.&#160; However, for
liabilities, SFAS No. 157 requires that a fair value measurement be the amount
that a company would pay to transfer a liability to a third party.&#160; Under previous practice, liabilities were
valued under a number of different methods.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SFAS No. 159 allows companies to measure specific financial assets and
liabilities at fair value, such as debt or equity investments.&#160;&#160; The fair value option for the investment in
Boston Scientific common stock was applied effective January 1, 2007.&#160; Abbott applied the fair value option to its
investment in Boston Scientific stock under SFAS No. 159 because, unlike its other
equity investments, the Boston Scientific stock is not a strategic investment
and Abbott is required to dispose of the stock no later than October 2008.&#160; Abbott was subject to a limitation on the
amount of shares it may sell in any one month through October 2007 and Abbott
will not reacquire the Boston Scientific shares it sells.&#160; Accordingly, since at adoption, realized
gains or losses were expected in the near future, the fair value option better
represented the near-term expected earnings impact from sales of the
stock.&#160;&#160; Under the fair value option, any
cumulative unrealized gains or losses on an equity investment previously
accounted for as an available-for-sale security is recorded as a cumulative
effect adjustment to retained earnings as of the date of adoption of the
standard.&#160; The pretax and after tax
adjustment to Earnings employed in the business upon adoption was $297 million
and $189 million, respectively, and the fair value and carrying amount of the
investment before and after adoption was $1.0 billion.&#160; The pretax and after tax adjustment to
Accumulated other comprehensive income was $303 million and $182 million,
respectively.&#160;&#160; The effect of the
adoption on deferred income taxes was not significant.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FASB Interpretation No.
48 requires that a recorded tax benefit must be more likely than not of being
sustained upon examination by tax authorities based upon its technical
merits.&#160; The amount of benefit recorded
is the largest amount of benefit that is greater than 50 percent likely of
being realized upon ultimate settlement.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to Condensed
Consolidated Financial Statements</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 45.0pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">September 30, 2007</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(Unaudited), continued</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 4 &#151; Business
Combinations and Related Transactions</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On April 21, 2006,
Abbott acquired Guidant&#146;s vascular intervention and endovascular solutions
businesses for approximately $4.1 billion, in cash, in connection with Boston
Scientific&#146;s acquisition of Guidant.&#160; In
addition, Abbott will also pay to Boston Scientific $250 million each upon
government approvals to market the <i>Xience</i>
<i>V </i>drug-eluting stent in the U.S.
and in Japan.&#160; Government approvals are
anticipated in 2008 for the U.S. and in 2009 for Japan.&#160; Each $250 million payment will result in
additional consideration for the acquisition of Guidant&#146;s vascular intervention
and endovascular solutions businesses.&#160;
The allocation of the purchase price as of September 30, 2006 resulted
in a charge of $665 million for acquired in-process research and development,
intangible assets of $1.2 billion, goodwill (primarily deductible) of $1.7
billion and tangible net assets of $580 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A substantial amount of the acquired
in-process research and development charge relating to the Guidant acquisition
related to drug eluting and bioabsorbable stents.&#160; The research efforts ranged from 35 percent
to 85 percent complete at the date of acquisition.&#160; The valuation method used to fair value the
projects was the Multi-period Excess Earnings Method (Income Approach) and the
risk-adjusted discount rates used ranged from 16 percent to 25 percent.&#160; In developing assumptions for the valuation
model, comparable Abbott products or products marketed by competitors were used
to estimate pricing, margins and expense levels.&#160; As of September 30, 2007, the research
efforts were primarily on schedule.&#160; The
estimated projected costs to complete totaled approximately $510 million as of
September 30, 2007, with anticipated product launch dates from 2008 through
2013.&#160; There have been no significant
changes in the development plans for the acquired incomplete projects.&#160; Significant net cash inflows will commence
within one to two years after product launch.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In order to
facilitate Boston Scientific&#146;s acquisition of Guidant, Abbott also acquired
64.6 million shares of Boston Scientific common stock directly from Boston
Scientific and loaned $900 million to a wholly-owned subsidiary of Boston
Scientific.&#160; The common stock was valued
at $1.3 billion and the note receivable was valued at $829 million at the acquisition
date.&#160; In connection with the acquisition
of the shares, Boston Scientific is entitled to certain after-tax gains upon
Abbott&#146;s sale of the shares.&#160; In
addition, Boston Scientific agreed to reimburse Abbott for certain borrowing
costs on debt incurred to acquire the Boston Scientific shares.&#160;&#160; Abbott recorded a net derivative financial
instruments liability of $59 million for the gain-sharing derivative financial
instrument liability and the interest derivative financial instrument asset.&#160; The effect of recording the shares, the loan
to Boston Scientific and the derivative financial instruments at fair value on
the date of acquisition resulted in the recording of additional goodwill of
approximately $204 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In December 2006, Abbott
acquired Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc. for cash of approximately $3.8 billion, net
of cash held by Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc.&#160;
The valuation of certain tangible assets and liabilities related to the
acquisition of Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc. is preliminary.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .7pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A charge of approximately $1.3 billion
for acquired in-process research and development was recorded relating to the
Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc. acquisition, which related primarily to cholesterol
treatment drugs.&#160; The research efforts
ranged from 70 percent to 80 percent complete at the date of acquisition.&#160; The valuation method used to fair value the
projects was the Multi-period Excess Earnings Method (Income Approach) and the
risk-adjusted discount rate used was 16 percent.&#160; In developing assumptions for the valuation
model, comparable Abbott products or products marketed by competitors were used
to estimate pricing, margins and expense levels.&#160; As of September 30, 2007, one drug was
approved for marketing in the U.S. and the remaining research efforts were
primarily on schedule.&#160; The estimated
projected costs to complete the projects totaled approximately $78 million as
of September 30, 2007 with anticipated product launches in 2008.&#160; There have been no significant changes in the
development plans for the acquired incomplete projects.&#160; Significant net cash inflows will commence
with the launches of the products.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(Unaudited), continued</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 5 &#151; Supplemental
Financial Information</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .45in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Other (income)
expense, net for the third quarter of 2007 includes a $35 million fair market
value loss adjustment to Abbott&#146;s investment in Boston Scientific common
stock.&#160; Other (income) expense, net for
the first nine months of 2007 includes a $136 million fair market value loss
adjustment to Abbott&#146;s investment in Boston Scientific common stock and a
realized gain of $37 million on the sales of Boston Scientific stock.&#160; Other (income) expense, net for the third
quarter and first nine months of 2006 includes fair value gain adjustments of
$23 million and $98 million, respectively, to certain derivative financial instruments
included with the investment in Boston Scientific common stock.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .45in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Investments at September
30, 2007 and December 31, 2006 consist of the following:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(dollars
in thousands)</font></i></p>

  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1,062,589</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:2.54%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;border:none;border-bottom:double windowtext 1.5pt;padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:1.92%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">$</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="13%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;border-bottom:double windowtext 1.5pt;border-left:none;border-right:none;border-top:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:13.1%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1,229,873</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:2.42%;">

</table>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 6 &#151; Taxes on
Earnings</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Taxes on earnings reflect the estimated annual
effective rates, including charges for interest and penalties, and the effect
of the resolution of prior years&#146; income tax audits in the third quarter 2006
and the effect of other discrete tax events that occurred in the second and
third quarters of 2006.&#160; For the nine
months ended September 30, 2006, 10.9 percentage points of tax benefit was
attributed to the income tax audit resolution and other discrete items,
primarily the tax benefit on acquired in-process and collaborations research
and development.&#160; The effective tax rates
are less than the statutory U.S. federal income tax rate principally due to the
domestic dividend exclusion and the benefit of lower statutory tax rates and
tax exemptions in several taxing jurisdictions.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Unrecognized tax benefits as of the adoption of FASB
Interpretation No. 48 on January 1, 2007 were approximately $579 million, which
if recognized, would decrease taxes on earnings.&#160; The total amount of unrecognized tax benefits
that, if recognized, would affect the effective tax rate in 2007 totaled
approximately <b>$</b>210 million.&#160; Due to the inherent uncertainties in tax
audits, Abbott is unable to estimate the range of reasonably possible change in
its unrecognized tax benefits, if any, within the next twelve months.&#160; Reserves for interest and penalties are not
significant.&#160; In the U.S., Abbott&#146;s
federal income tax returns through 2003 are settled, and the income tax returns
for years after 2003 are open.&#160; There are
numerous other income tax jurisdictions for which tax returns are not yet
settled, none of which are individually significant.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to Condensed
Consolidated Financial Statements</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 45.0pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">September 30, 2007</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(Unaudited), continued</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 7 &#151;
Litigation and Environmental Matters</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Abbott
has been identified as a potentially responsible party for investigation and
cleanup costs at a number of locations in the United States and Puerto Rico
under federal and state remediation laws and is investigating potential
contamination at a number of company-owned locations.&#160; Abbott has recorded an estimated cleanup cost
for each site for which management believes Abbott has a probable loss
exposure.&#160; No individual site cleanup exposure
is expected to exceed $3&nbsp;million, and the aggregate cleanup exposure is not
expected to exceed $15&nbsp;million.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">There are a number of patent
disputes with third parties who claim Abbott&#146;s products infringe their
patents.&nbsp; In one dispute, which Abbott assumed as part of the Guidant
acquisition, reserves equal to the expected resolution have been recorded.&#160; In another dispute, filed in April 2007,
Abbott is unable to estimate a range of possible loss, if any, and no reserve
has been recorded.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">There
are several civil actions pending brought by individuals or entities that
allege generally that Abbott and numerous pharmaceutical companies reported
false or misleading pricing information relating to the average wholesale price
of certain pharmaceutical products in connection with federal, state and
private reimbursement.&#160; Civil actions
have also been brought against Abbott, and in some cases other members of the
pharmaceutical industry, by state attorneys general seeking to recover alleged
damages on behalf of state Medicaid programs.&#160;
In May 2006, Abbott was notified that the U.S. Department of Justice
intervened in a civil whistle-blower lawsuit alleging that Abbott inflated
prices for Medicaid and Medicare reimbursable drugs.&#160; The outcome of these investigations and
litigation could include the imposition of fines or penalties.&#160; Abbott is unable to estimate the amount of
possible loss, and no loss reserves have been recorded for these
exposures.&#160; Many of the products involved
in these cases are Hospira products.&#160;
Hospira, Abbott&#146;s former hospital products business, was spun off to
Abbott&#146;s shareholders in 2004.&#160; Abbott
retained liability for losses that result from these cases and investigations
to the extent any such losses both relate to the sale of Hospira&#146;s products
prior to the spin-off of Hospira and relate to allegations that were made in
such pending and future cases and investigations that were the same as
allegations existing at the date of the spin-off.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Within
the next year, legal proceedings may occur that may result in a change in the
estimated reserves recorded by Abbott.&nbsp; For its legal proceedings and
environmental exposures, except as noted in the second and third paragraphs of
this footnote, Abbott estimates the range of possible loss to be from
approximately $180 million to $325 million.&#160;
The recorded reserve balance at September 30, 2007 for these proceedings
and exposures was approximately $215 million.&nbsp; These reserves represent
management&#146;s best estimate of probable loss, as defined by Statement of
Financial Accounting Standards No.&nbsp;5, &#147;Accounting for Contingencies.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">While
it is not feasible to predict the outcome of all such proceedings and exposures
with certainty, management believes that their ultimate disposition should not
have a material adverse effect on Abbott&#146;s financial position, cash flows, or
results of operations, except for the cases and investigations discussed in the
third paragraph of this footnote, the resolution of which could be material to
cash flows or results of operations for a quarter.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">8</font></p>

<div style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Abbott
funds its domestic defined benefit plans according to IRS funding
limitations.&#160; In the first quarters of
2007 and 2006, $200 was contributed to the main domestic defined benefit plan
and $75 and $40, respectively, was contributed to the post-employment medical
and dental benefit plans.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 10 &#151; Segment Information</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">(dollars in millions)</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 17.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .7pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Abbott&#146;s principal
business is the discovery, development, manufacture and sale of a broad line of
health care products.&#160; Abbott&#146;s products
are generally sold directly to retailers, wholesalers, hospitals, health care
facilities, laboratories, physicians&#146; offices and government agencies
throughout the world.&#160; Abbott&#146;s
reportable segments are as follows:</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to Condensed
Consolidated Financial Statements</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 45.0pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">September 30, 2007</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(Unaudited), continued</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Pharmaceutical
Products</font></i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> &#151;
Worldwide sales of a broad line of pharmaceuticals.&#160; For segment reporting purposes, two
pharmaceutical divisions are aggregated and reported as the Pharmaceutical
Products segment.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 45.0pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Nutritional
Products</font></i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;<font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">  </font>Worldwide sales of a broad line of adult
and pediatric nutritional products.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Diagnostic
Products</font></i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">  </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;<font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">  </font>Worldwide sales of diagnostic systems and
tests for blood banks, hospitals, commercial laboratories and alternate-care
testing sites.&#160; For segment reporting
purposes, three diagnostic divisions are aggregated and reported as the
Diagnostic Products segment.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Vascular</font></i><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">  <i>Products</i><font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">&nbsp;</font>&#151;<font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;">  </font>Worldwide
sales of coronary, endovascular and vessel closure products.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 26.65pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Abbott&#146;s underlying accounting records are maintained
on a legal entity basis for government and public reporting requirements.&#160; Segment disclosures are on a performance
basis consistent with internal management reporting.&#160; Intersegment transfers of inventory are
recorded at standard cost and are not a measure of segment operating
earnings.&#160; The cost of some corporate
functions and the cost of certain employee benefits are charged to segments at
predetermined rates that approximate cost.&#160;
Remaining costs, if any, are not allocated to segments<b>.&#160; </b>Effective
in the second quarter of 2007, the Diagnostic segment was reorganized.&#160; Prior period segment information has been
adjusted to reflect this change.&#160; For
acquisitions prior to 2006, substantially all intangible assets and related
amortization are not allocated to segments.<b>&#160; </b>The following segment information
has been prepared in accordance with the internal accounting policies of
Abbott, as described above, and are not presented in accordance with generally
accepted accounting principles applied to the consolidated financial
statements.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 17.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt .5in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The decrease in Nutritional Products segment operating
earnings for the three and nine months ended September 30, 2007 was due to the
completion of the U.S. co-promotion of <i>Synagis</i>
in 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt .5in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The increase in Vascular Product segment sales for the
nine months ended September 30, 2007, is primarily due to the acquisition of
Guidant&#146;s vascular intervention and endovascular solutions businesses on April
21, 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt .5in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Sales from the diabetes, bulk pharmaceuticals, spine
and animal health businesses are included in Other sales.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt .5in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Other, net for the three months and nine months ended
September 30, 2007, includes acquisition integration expenses related to the
acquisitions of Guidant&#146;s vascular intervention and endovascular solutions
businesses and Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc., fair market value loss adjustments to
Abbott&#146;s investment in Boston Scientific common stock and </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the cost of
terminating a contract</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">.&#160;&#160; Other, net for the three months ended
September 30, 2007, also includes the reinstatement of depreciation and
amortization on assets that were classified as held for sale that was suspended
as of January 17, 2007.&#160; This
depreciation and amortization was recorded in the third quarter of 2007, as
these operations were no longer classified as held for sale as of July 11,
2007.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10</font></p>

<p align="left" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 5.4pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">The total unrecognized compensation cost related to all share-based
compensation plans at September 30, 2007, amounted to approximately $321
million which is expected to be recognized over the next three years.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 45.0pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 12 &#151; Equity Method Investment</font></p>

in millions)</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">Note&nbsp;13&nbsp;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#151;<font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;"> Goodwill and Intangible Assets</font></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">(dollars in millions)</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">Foreign currency translation adjustments and other
adjustments increased goodwill in the first nine months of 2007 and 2006 by
approximately $222<b>  </b>and $322, respectively.&#160; Abbott recorded total goodwill of
approximately $1,900 related to the acquisition of </font><font face="Times New Roman">Guidant&#146;s
vascular intervention and endovascular solutions businesses<font style="letter-spacing:-.1pt;"> in the second quarter of 2006.&#160; There were no reductions of goodwill relating
to impairments or disposal of all or a portion of a business.&#160; </font>The amount of goodwill related to
reportable segments at September 30, 2007 was $5,748 for the Pharmaceutical
Products segment, $201 for the Nutritional Products segment, $262 for the
Diagnostics Products segment and $1,970 for the Vascular Products segment.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">The
gross amount of amortizable intangible assets, primarily product rights and
technology was $9,023<b>  </b>as of
September 30, 2007 and $8,988 as of December&nbsp;31, 2006, and accumulated
amortization was $3,171 as of September 30, 2007 and $2,602 as of December 31,
2006.&#160; The estimated annual amortization
expense for intangible assets is $765<b>  </b>in
2007, $705 in 2008, $708 in 2009, $709 in 2010 and $689 in 2011.&#160; Intangible assets are amortized primarily on
a straight-line basis over 1 to 25&nbsp;years (average 11&nbsp;years).</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to Condensed
Consolidated Financial Statements</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 45.0pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">September 30, 2007</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(Unaudited), continued</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .5in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Note 14 &#151;
Restructuring Plans</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;letter-spacing:-.1pt;">(dollars in millions)</font></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in .5in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
2007, 2006 and 2005, Abbott management approved plans to realign its worldwide
pharmaceutical manufacturing operations and selected domestic and international
commercial and research and development operations in order to reduce costs.&#160; Additional charges of $77 and $39 were
subsequently recorded in the first nine months of 2007 and 2006, respectively,
relating to these restructurings, primarily for accelerated depreciation.&#160; In addition, Abbott implemented facilities
restructuring plans in the second quarter of 2007 related to the acquired
operations of Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc., which resulted in an increase to
goodwill of approximately $52.&#160; The
following summarizes the activity for restructurings:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr>
  <td width="61%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:61.92%;">
  <p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 10.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-10.0pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
  </td>
  <td width="3%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:3.7%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<div>

<p align="center" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to Condensed
Consolidated Financial Statements</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 45.0pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">September 30, 2007</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(Unaudited), continued</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following
table summarizes the activity for the gain sharing derivative financial
instrument liability.&#160; The adjustment to
record this liability at fair value has been recorded in Other (income)
expense, net for the nine months ended September 30, 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:left;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For assets and
liabilities that are measured using quoted prices in active markets, the total
fair value is the published market price per unit multiplied by the number of
units held without consideration of transaction costs.&#160; Assets and liabilities that are measured
using significant other observable inputs are valued by reference to similar
assets or liabilities, adjusted for contract restrictions and other terms
specific to that asset or liability.&#160; For
these items, a significant portion of fair value is derived by reference to
quoted prices of similar assets or liabilities in active markets.&#160; For all remaining assets and liabilities,
fair value is derived using a fair value model, such as a discounted cash flow
model or Black-Scholes model.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 24.0pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-24.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; The Pharmaceutical Products segment had an
agreement with Boehringer Ingelheim (BI) to co-promote and distribute three of
its products in the U.S. In 2005, Abbott and BI amended the agreement and
effective January 1, 2006, Abbott no longer distributed or recorded sales for
distribution activities for the BI products, although Abbott recorded a small
amount of co-promotion revenue in the first quarter of 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Worldwide 2007
sales compared to 2006 reflect the acquisitions of Guidant&#146;s vascular
intervention and endovascular solutions businesses on April 21, 2006 and Kos
Pharmaceuticals Inc. in the fourth quarter of 2006. The sales growth in 2007
also reflects unit growth and the positive effect of the relatively weaker U.S.
dollar.&#160; The relatively weaker U.S.
dollar increased third quarter 2007 consolidated net sales by 2.8 percent,
Total International sales by 5.7 percent, Pharmaceutical Products segment sales
by 3.0 percent and Diagnostic Products segment sales by 3.9 percent over the
third quarter of 2006.&#160; The relatively
weaker U.S. dollar also increased the first nine months 2007 consolidated net
sales by 2.7 percent, Total International sales by 5.5 percent, Pharmaceutical
Products segment sales by 2.8 percent and Diagnostic Products segment sales by
3.9 percent over the first nine months of 2006.&#160;
The sales growth for the third quarter and nine months 2006 compared to
2005, excluding sales of BI products, reflects the acquisition of Guidant&#146;s
vascular intervention and endovascular solutions businesses on April 21, 2006.
The sales growth in 2006 also reflects unit growth and the effects of exchange.&#160; The relatively weaker U.S. dollar increased
third quarter 2006 consolidated net sales by 0.9 percent, Total International
sales by 2.1 percent, Pharmaceutical Products segment sales by 0.9 percent and
Diagnostic Products segment sales by 1.3 percent over the third quarter of
2005. The relatively stronger U.S. dollar decreased the first nine months 2006
consolidated net sales by 0.9 percent, Total International sales by 2.0
percent, Pharmaceutical Products segment sales by 1.0 percent and Diagnostic
Products segment sales by 1.7 percent over the first nine months of 2005.&#160; Sales growth in 2007 for the Nutritional
Products segment was unfavorably impacted by the completion of the U.S.
co-promotion of <i>Synagis </i>in 2006.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">14</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

  <td width="344" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="14" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="12" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="77" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="20" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="81" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="26" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="12" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="54" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="11" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="75" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="12" style="border:none;"></td>
  <td width="4" style="border:none;"></td>

<p style="margin:0in .5in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased sales of <i>HUMIRA</i> and <i>Depakote</i> accounted for the majority of the sales increase
for U.S. Specialty products in both 2007 and 2006.&#160; U.S. sales of <i>HUMIRA</i> were $1.1 billion, $806 million and $568 million for
the nine months ended September 30, 2007, 2006 and 2005, respectively.&#160; U.S. Primary Care sales in 2007 were
favorably impacted by sales of <i>Niaspan</i>,
a new product from the acquisition of Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc. in the fourth
quarter of 2006.&#160; U.S. Primary Care sales
were also favorably impacted by increased sales of <i>TriCor</i> in both periods and were unfavorably impacted by
decreased sales of <i>Omnicef</i> in
2007 and <i>Biaxin</i> in 2007 and 2006
due to the introduction of generic competition.&#160;
Sales of <i>Omnicef</i> were $225
million and $378 million for the nine months ended September 30, 2007 and 2006,
respectively, and sales of <i>Biaxin</i>
were $21 million, $95 million and $213 million for the nine months ended
September 30, 2007, 2006 and 2005, respectively.&#160;&#160; Increased sales of <i>HUMIRA</i> favorably impacted International
Pharmaceutical sales in 2007 and 2006.&#160;
International sales of <i>HUMIRA</i>
were $986 million, $617 million and $392 million for the nine months ended
September 30, 2007, 2006 and 2005, respectively.&#160; The relatively weaker U.S. dollar increased
International Pharmaceutical sales by 5.9 percent in 2007 and the relatively
stronger U.S. dollar decreased International Pharmaceutical sales by 2.4
percent in 2006.&#160; The decrease in sales
of U.S. Pediatric Nutritional sales in 2006 was due to overall infant
nutritionals non-WIC category decline and competitive share loss.&#160; International Pediatric Nutritionals sales
increases in 2007 and 2006 were due primarily to volume growth in developing
countries.&#160; The relatively weaker U.S.
dollar increased Immunochemistry sales by 4.2 percent in 2007 and the
relatively stronger U.S. dollar decreased Immunochemistry sales by 1.9 percent
in 2006.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The gross profit
margin was 55.1 percent for the
third quarter 2007, compared to 57.1 percent for the third quarter 2006.&#160; First nine months 2007 gross profit margin
was 55.8 percent, compared to 57.3 percent for the first nine months 2006.&#160; The decreases in the gross profit margins in
2007 were due, in part, to the effect of the unfavorable impact in 2007 from
the completion of the U.S. co-promotion of <i>Synagis</i>
in 2006 as well as generic competition for <i>Omnicef</i>
and <i>Biaxin</i> sales in 2007.&#160; Increased amortization of intangible assets
acquired in 2006 also had an unfavorable impact on the gross profit margins in
2007.&#160; As discussed below, the
reinstatement in the third quarter 2007 of the suspended depreciation and
amortization for the operations that were classified as held for sale also
unfavorably impacted the gross profit margin in the third quarter of 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Research and
development expenses increased 3.7
percent in the third quarter 2007 and 11.1
percent for the first nine months 2007 over comparable 2006 periods.&#160; These increases reflect the effect of the
acquisitions of Guidant&#146;s vascular intervention and endovascular solutions businesses
on April 21, 2006 and Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc. in the fourth quarter of
2006.&#160; These increases also reflect
increased spending to support pipeline programs, including new indications for <i>HUMIRA,</i> and ABT-335 (a cholesterol drug),
ABT-335/Crestor fixed-dose combination, ABT-874 (a psoriasis drug),
controlled-release <i>Vicodin </i>and <i>Xience V, </i>as well as several Phase I and
Phase II clinical programs in neuroscience and oncology.&#160; The majority of research and development
expenditures is concentrated on pharmaceutical products.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">15</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FINANCIAL REVIEW</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 1.1pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(continued)</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Selling, general
and administrative expenses for the third quarter and first nine months 2007
increased 17.1 percent and 19.0 percent, respectively, over the
comparable 2006 periods.&#160;&#160; These
increases reflect the effect of the acquisitions of Guidant&#146;s vascular
intervention and endovascular solutions businesses on April 21, 2006 and Kos
Pharmaceuticals Inc. in the fourth quarter of 2006.&#160; The increases also reflect increased selling
and marketing support for new and existing products, including continued
spending for <i>HUMIRA </i>and the
continuing international launch of <i>Xience V</i>,
as well as spending on other marketed pharmaceutical products.&#160; In
the third quarter of 2007, Abbott terminated a contract that resulted in a
third quarter charge to selling, general and administrative expenses of $92
million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Reclassification
of Assets Previously Classified as Held for Sale</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;vertical-align:baseline;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman"><font style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">On January 17, 2007, the date that
Abbott agreed to sell its core laboratory diagnostics businesses to GE, </font>the
assets of the operations held for sale and the liabilities to be assumed in the
intended sale were classified as held for sale</font><font color="black"><font style="color:windowtext;"> and depreciation of
property and equipment and amortization of intangible assets was
discontinued.&#160; </font>On July 11, 2007,
Abbott announced that Abbott and GE mutually agreed to terminate the contract
to sell Abbott&#146;s core laboratory diagnostics business to GE.&#160; The assets of the operations previously held
for sale and the liabilities to be assumed in the intended sale have been
reclassified to assets held and used.&#160;
Accordingly, </font><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">depreciation and amortization that was discontinued in
the amount of approximately $99 million has been recorded in the third quarter
of 2007.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Restructurings</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(<i>dollars in millions</i>)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In
2007, 2006 and 2005, Abbott management approved plans to realign its worldwide
pharmaceutical manufacturing operations and selected domestic and international
commercial and research and development operations in order to reduce
costs.&#160; Additional charges of $77 and $39
were subsequently recorded in the first nine months of 2007 and 2006,
respectively, relating to these restructurings, primarily for accelerated
depreciation.&#160; In addition, Abbott
implemented facilities restructuring plans in the second quarter of 2007
related to the acquired operations of Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc., which resulted
in an increase to goodwill of approximately $52.&#160; The following summarizes the activity for
restructurings:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">FINANCIAL REVIEW</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 1.1pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(continued)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Business Combinations and Related Transactions</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On April 21, 2006,
Abbott acquired Guidant&#146;s vascular intervention and endovascular solutions
businesses for approximately $4.1 billion, in cash, in connection with Boston
Scientific&#146;s acquisition of Guidant.&#160; In
addition, Abbott will also pay to Boston Scientific $250 million each upon
government approvals to market the <i>Xience</i>
<i>V </i>drug-eluting stent in the U.S.
and in Japan.&#160; Government approvals are
anticipated in 2008 for the U.S. and in 2009 for Japan.&#160; Each $250 million payment will result in
additional consideration for the acquisition of Guidant&#146;s vascular intervention
and endovascular solutions businesses.&#160;
The allocation of the purchase price as of September 30, 2006 resulted
in a charge of $665 million for acquired in-process research and development,
intangible assets of $1.2 billion, goodwill (primarily deductible) of $1.7
billion and tangible net assets of $580 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A substantial amount of the acquired
in-process research and development charge relating to the Guidant acquisition
related to drug eluting and bioabsorbable stents.&#160; The research efforts ranged from 35 percent
to 85 percent complete at the date of acquisition.&#160; The valuation method used to fair value the
projects was the Multi-period Excess Earnings Method (Income Approach) and the
risk-adjusted discount rates used ranged from 16 percent to 25 percent.&#160; In developing assumptions for the valuation
model, comparable Abbott products or products marketed by competitors were used
to estimate pricing, margins and expense levels.&#160; As of September 30, 2007, the research
efforts were primarily on schedule.&#160; The
estimated projected costs to complete totaled approximately $510 million as of
September 30, 2007, with anticipated product launch dates from 2008 through
2013.&#160; There have been no significant
changes in the development plans for the acquired incomplete projects.&#160; Significant net cash inflows will commence
within one to two years after product launch.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .2in .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In order to
facilitate Boston Scientific&#146;s acquisition of Guidant, Abbott also acquired
64.6 million shares of Boston Scientific common stock directly from Boston
Scientific and loaned $900 million to a wholly-owned subsidiary of Boston
Scientific.&#160; The common stock was valued
at $1.3 billion and the note receivable was valued at $829 million at the
acquisition date.&#160; In connection with the
acquisition of the shares, Boston Scientific is entitled to certain after-tax
gains upon Abbott&#146;s sale of the shares.&#160;
In addition, Boston Scientific agreed to reimburse Abbott for certain
borrowing costs on debt incurred to acquire the Boston Scientific shares.&#160;&#160; Abbott recorded a net derivative financial
instruments liability of $59 million for the gain-sharing derivative financial
instrument liability and the interest derivative financial instrument
asset.&#160; The effect of recording the
shares, the loan to Boston Scientific and the derivative financial instruments
at fair value on the date of acquisition resulted in the recording of
additional goodwill of approximately $204 million.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In December 2006, Abbott
acquired Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc. for cash of approximately $3.8 billion, net
of cash held by Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc.&#160;
The valuation of certain tangible assets and liabilities related to the
acquisition of Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc. is preliminary.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .7pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A charge of approximately $1.3 billion
for acquired in-process research and development was recorded relating to the
Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc. acquisition, which related primarily to cholesterol
treatment drugs.&#160; The research efforts
ranged from 70 percent to 80 percent complete at the date of acquisition.&#160; The valuation method used to fair value the
projects was the Multi-period Excess Earnings Method (Income Approach) and the
risk-adjusted discount rate used was 16 percent.&#160; In developing assumptions for the valuation
model, comparable Abbott products or products marketed by competitors were used
to estimate pricing, margins and expense levels.&#160; As of September 30, 2007, one drug was approved
for marketing in the U.S. and the remaining research efforts were primarily on
schedule.&#160; The estimated projected costs
to complete the projects totaled approximately $78 million as of September 30,
2007 with anticipated product launches in 2008.&#160;
There have been no significant changes in the development plans for the
acquired incomplete projects.&#160;
Significant net cash inflows will commence with the launches of the
products.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 62.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 44.3pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Interest expense</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in .9pt .0001pt 0in;punctuation-wrap:simple;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Interest expense
increased in the third quarter and first nine months of 2007 due primarily to
higher borrowings as a result of the acquisitions of Guidant&#146;s vascular
intervention and endovascular solutions businesses and Kos Pharmaceuticals Inc.
and Abbott&#146;s investment in the Boston Scientific common stock and note
receivable.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">17</font></p>
